Playing to Lose	Dracnomicon	110	Rule		AD&D	VR	Played at the beginning of the player's turn, this card is not discarded. While this rule is in effect, the first player to have six razed realms in his formation for one full turn wins, instead of the normal winning conditions. Players may attack razed realms in another player's formation to discard them, if successful.
